posted:Posted July 10, 2023
msg:Because of well-known reasons, the hotel market in Beijing was particularly hot this summer, so when I saw the price of the parent-child suite in this hotel, I thought it was quite reasonable. When my wife saw that the hotel had bad reviews and persuaded me to change rooms, I dismissed it on the grounds that the room was good, but later facts proved that I had made a very bad choice.
When I arrived at the hotel, I found that it seemed to be the Beijing Office of Jilin Province. In fact, this was the reason for everything that happened, because no matter how bad the service was, they did not lack customers, and the demand from the province could already feed them.
Let‚Äôs talk about how terrible this hotel is in detail. The following are the terrible things that happened in chronological order.

1. The hotel facilities are old and poorly maintained. On the day we moved in, we discovered that the water pipe under the sink was separated from the sink, and water leaked all over the floor. After waiting for a long time, the engineering staff came and said it was repaired in 10 seconds. When I used water at night, I found that it was still leaking, so I repaired it again before it was repaired. In addition, there are very few plugs in the room, and charging mobile phones and watches is very troublesome.

2 breakfasts. The breakfast management of this restaurant is the worst I have ever seen. No matter what time you go, there are always only one or two breads. If you ask the waiter, the waiter will tell you that they are gone. The latte produced by the coffee machine is only about 50ml each time. If you want to make a normal cup, you can only make it three times. The screen always shows that it needs maintenance and cleaning, but the waiter will tell you that it is okay, that's it. The knife my son asked the waiter for was actually used. The old lady next door to me ate some scraps of steel wire used to clean the pot in her dish. The waiter looked at it and threw it on the floor, said sorry and left.

3. The management is chaotic. On the day I checked in, the hotel staff did not ask me for a deposit. I thought it was Ctrip's check-out payment, so I didn't pay attention. After we added a children's meal to breakfast the next day, the hotel probably discovered that I didn't have a deposit for my room, so when we were visiting the Great Wall, the hotel called me and asked me if I had checked out? After learning that there was another reservation for our room, we asked if our luggage was in the room? I told them that all the luggage was in the room, so the front desk said that we didn't have the deposit and asked us to go to the front desk to pay the deposit when we went back. There was a misunderstanding here. At that time, the deposit was not enough because of the extra buffet breakfast, so I promised to go to the front desk to handle it when I returned. When we returned to the hotel exhausted from the Great Wall, our first thought was to go back to the room to take a shower. When we arrived at the room door and swiped the card to open the door, we found that both key cards were not working. At this time, the cleaning staff told us that the hotel front desk They demagnetized our key cards and asked us to go to the front desk. We asked the housekeeper to open the door first and wait until we finished taking a shower, but the housekeeper said that the front desk would not let her open it and that we had to let us go down. So we called the front desk and sent the message. After a fuss, the cleaning lady opened the door.

Later, when I recalled the previous call from the front desk, I realized that when she asked if our luggage was in the room, she wanted to make sure that she had locked the door to ensure that we could not escape or default on our account. This kind of behavior of treating customers as thieves is really shocking.

4. None of the staff will say hello to you, even if you say it firstüò°

In short, anyone who thinks that he may be luckier than me and will not catch up with me can refer to everything our family has experienced. I have 100% reason to be sure that what happened to us is not just What happened to us will definitely happen to any hotel guest.
